reminderLocalDueTime = new Date(year, month - 1, day, hour, minute); if (isNaN(reminderLocalDueTime.getTime())) { throw new Error("Invalid date/time components"); } if (reminderLocalDueTime <= now) { isOverdue = true; } } } else if (reminder.isLocationEnabled && reminder.locationCoordinates && currentCoords) { // Proximity check for faster polling even if not overdue yet const distance = calculateDistance( currentCoords.latitude, currentCoords.longitude, reminder.locationCoordinates.latitude, reminder.locationCoordinates.longitude ); } }); if (storageNeedsUpdate) { try { const oldStorageString = localStorage.getItem('reminders') || '[]'; const newStorageString = JSON.stringify(validRemindersForStorage); if (oldStorageString !== newStorageString) { localStorage.setItem('reminders', newStorageString); } } catch (e) { showToast("Error al actualizar recordatorios tras limpieza.", "error", 5000); } } if (overdueReminders.length > 0) { if (!isUnifiedWindowVisibleByLogic || newOverdueFound) { currentNotificationSlideIndex = 0; } else { nextSlideIndex = 0; // Stay on the single slide } if (totalSlides === 1 || nextSlideIndex !== currentNotificationSlideIndex) { currentNotificationSlideIndex = nextSlideIndex; const targetScrollLeft = currentNotificationSlideIndex * swiperContainer.offsetWidth; if (firstTabButton) { firstTabButton.click(); } } function parseCoordinateFilter(inputValue) { const cleanedValue = inputValue.trim(); if (!cleanedValue) return { type: 'empty' }; const parts = cleanedValue.split(/\s+/).map(p => parseFloat(p)); if (parts.some(isNaN)) return { type: 'error', message: 'Contiene valores no numéricos.' }; if (parts.length === 1) { return { type: 'single', value: parts[0] }; } else if (parts.length === 2) { return { type: 'range', min: Math.min(parts[0], parts[1]), max: Math.max(parts[0], parts[1]) }; } else { return { type: 'error', message: 'Demasiados valores. Usar 1 o 2.' }; } } async function handleImportRadars() { const importExtraCheckbox = document.getElementById('import-extra-radars-checkbox'); const KML_FILES_LIST_STANDARD = './KLM/KLMFILES.TXT'; const KML_FILES_LIST_EXTRA = './KLM/KLMFILES2.TXT'; const KML_FILES_LIST_PATH = importExtraCheckbox.checked ? let passesLatFilter = true; if (latFilterParsed.type === 'single') { passesLatFilter = Math.abs(lat - latFilterParsed.value) < 0.0001; } else if (latFilterParsed.type === 'range') { passesLatFilter = lat >= latFilterParsed.min && lat <= latFilterParsed.max; } if (!passesLatFilter) continue; let passesLonFilter = true; if (lonFilterParsed.type === 'single') { passesLonFilter = Math.abs(lon - lonFilterParsed.value) < 0.0001; } else if (lonFilterParsed.type === 'range') { passesLonFilter = lon >= lonFilterParsed.min && lon <= lonFilterParsed.max; } let matchesLat = latFilterParsed.type === 'empty'; if (latFilterParsed.type === 'single') { matchesLat = Math.abs(reminder.locationCoordinates.latitude - latFilterParsed.value) < 0.0001; } else if (latFilterParsed.type === 'range') { matchesLat = reminder.locationCoordinates.latitude >= latFilterParsed.min && reminder.locationCoordinates.latitude <= latFilterParsed.max; } if (matchesLat && matchesLon && matchesKeywords) { deletedCount++; return false; } return true; }); if (deletedCount > 0) { localStorage.setItem('reminders', JSON.stringify(remindersToKeep)); if (!isMobile) showToast(`${deletedCount} recordatorios borrados.`, 'success'); if(progressStatus) progressStatus.textContent = "No se encontraron coincidencias."; } } const sleep = ms => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms)); function showToast(message, type = 'info', duration = 3000) { const existingToast = document.getElementById('toast-notification-element'); } }, { once: true }); }, duration); } function formatDateToDDMMMYY(dateString) { if (!dateString) return '-'; try { const [year, month, day] = dateString.split('-').map(Number); const date = new Date(Date.UTC(year, month - 1, day)); if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return '-'; const dayOfMonth = String(date.getUTCDate()).padStart(2, '0'); const monthNames = ['Ene', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Abr', 'May', 'Jun', 'Jul', 'Ago', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dic']; const monthName = monthNames[date.getUTCMonth()]; const yearShort = String(date.getUTCFullYear()).slice(-2); return `${dayOfMonth} ${monthName} ${yearShort}`; } catch (e) { return '-'; } } function formatDateDetailed(dateString) { if (!dateString || !dateString.match(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/)) return '-'; try { const [year, month, day] = dateString.split('-').map(Number); const date = new Date(Date.UTC(year, month - 1, day)); if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return dateString; const dayOfMonth = String(date.getUTCDate()).padStart(2, '0'); const monthNames = ['Enero', 'Febrero', 'Marzo', 'Abril', 'Mayo', 'Junio', 'Julio', 'Agosto', 'Septiembre', 'Octubre', 'Noviembre', 'Diciembre']; const monthName = monthNames[date.getUTCMonth()]; const fullYear = date.getUTCFullYear(); return `${dayOfMonth}-${monthName}-${fullYear}`; } catch (e) { return dateString; } } function formatTimeWithPeriod(timeString) { if (!timeString || !timeString.match(/^\d{2}:\d{2}$/)) return '-'; try { const [hourStr, minuteStr] = timeString.split(':'); const hour = parseInt(hourStr); const minute = parseInt(minuteStr); if (isNaN(hour) || isNaN(minute) || hour < 0 || hour > 23 || minute < 0 || minute > 59) { return timeString; } let period = ''; if (hour >= 22 || hour < 5) { period = 'de la Noche'; } else if (hour >= 5 && hour < 12) { period = 'de la Mañana'; } else if (hour >= 12 && hour < 14) { period = 'del Mediodía'; } else { period = 'de la Tarde'; } return `${hourStr}:${minuteStr} (${period})`; } catch (e) { return timeString; } } let globalModalTimers = {}; function addModalAutoCloseTimer(modalElement, closeButtonElement, modalId, duration = 60000) { if (!modalElement || !closeButtonElement || !modalId) { return; } modalElement.dataset.modalTimerId = modalId; clearModalAutoCloseTimer(modalElement, closeButtonElement, modalId); let countdown = duration / 1000; const originalButtonText = closeButtonElement.textContent.split(' (')[0]; const countdownSpanId = `modal-countdown-${modalId}`; let countdownSpan = closeButtonElement.querySelector(`.button-countdown-timer`); if (!countdownSpan) { countdownSpan = document.createElement('span'); countdownSpan.className = 'button-countdown-timer'; countdownSpan.style.marginLeft = '5px'; countdownSpan.style.fontWeight = 'normal'; closeButtonElement.appendChild(countdownSpan); } countdownSpan.textContent = ` (${countdown})`; const intervalId = setInterval(() => { countdown--; if (countdownSpan && document.body.contains(countdownSpan)) { countdownSpan.textContent = ` (${countdown})`; } if (countdown <= 0) { if (globalModalTimers[modalId]) { clearInterval(globalModalTimers[modalId].intervalId); delete globalModalTimers[modalId]; } if (closeButtonElement && document.body.contains(closeButtonElement)) { closeButtonElement.click(); } else if (modalElement && modalElement.parentNode) { modalElement.parentNode.removeChild(modalElement); } } }, 1000); const resetTimerHandler = () => { if (!globalModalTimers[modalId] || !globalModalTimers[modalId].intervalId) return; clearInterval(globalModalTimers[modalId].intervalId); countdown = duration / 1000; if (countdownSpan && document.body.contains(countdownSpan)) { countdownSpan.textContent = ` (${countdown})`; } const newIntervalId = setInterval(() => { countdown--; if (countdownSpan && document.body.contains(countdownSpan)) { countdownSpan.textContent = ` (${countdown})`; } if (countdown <= 0) { if (globalModalTimers[modalId]) { clearInterval(globalModalTimers[modalId].intervalId); delete globalModalTimers[modalId]; } if (closeButtonElement && document.body.contains(closeButtonElement)) { closeButtonElement.click(); } else if (modalElement && modalElement.parentNode) { modalElement.parentNode.removeChild(modalElement); } } }, 1000); globalModalTimers[modalId].intervalId = newIntervalId; }; modalElement.addEventListener('click', resetTimerHandler); modalElement.addEventListener('touchstart', resetTimerHandler, { passive: true }); modalElement.addEventListener('input', resetTimerHandler); modalElement.addEventListener('scroll', resetTimerHandler, { passive: true }); globalModalTimers[modalId] = { intervalId: intervalId, resetHandler: resetTimerHandler, modalElement: modalElement, closeButtonElement: closeButtonElement, countdownSpan: countdownSpan }; } function clearModalAutoCloseTimer(modalElement, closeButtonElement, modalId) { const timerIdToClear = modalId || (modalElement ? modalElement.dataset.modalTimerId : null); if (timerIdToClear && globalModalTimers[timerIdToClear]) { clearInterval(globalModalTimers[timerIdToClear].intervalId); const timerData = globalModalTimers[timerIdToClear]; if (timerData.modalElement && timerData.resetHandler) { timerData.modalElement.removeEventListener('click', timerData.resetHandler); timerData.modalElement.removeEventListener('touchstart', timerData.resetHandler); timerData.modalElement.removeEventListener('input', timerData.resetHandler); timerData.modalElement.removeEventListener('scroll', timerData.resetHandler); } if (timerData.countdownSpan && timerData.countdownSpan.parentNode) { timerData.countdownSpan.remove(); } delete globalModalTimers[timerIdToClear]; } if(closeButtonElement){ const orphanSpans = closeButtonElement.querySelectorAll('.button-countdown-timer'); orphanSpans.forEach(s => s.remove()); } if(modalElement && modalElement.dataset.modalTimerId) { delete modalElement.dataset.modalTimerId; } } // --- Navigation Functions --- function showNavigationRouteModal() { // Close any other modals hideUnifiedReminderWindow(); const otherModals = document.querySelectorAll('.choice-modal, .edit-modal, .edit-info-modal, .help-modal, .reminder-modal, .reminder-table-modal, #postpone-options-modal, .versions-modal-overlay, .saved-locations-modal, #reminders-location-map-modal, #reminders-map-help-modal-instance, #saved-routes-modal'); otherModals.forEach(m => { if (m.id === 'reminders-location-map-modal') { // Special handling for radar map to ensure watch is cleared const mapModalElement = document.getElementById('reminders-location-map-modal'); if (mapModalElement) { const closeButton = mapModalElement.querySelector('#close-reminders-location-map'); if (closeButton) closeButton.click(); // Use the click handler to ensure cleanup } } else { m.remove(); } }); const navModal = document.getElementById('navigation-route-modal'); navModal.style.display = 'flex'; if (!navigationMapInstance) { initializeNavigationMap('navigation-map-div'); } else { // If map exists, just make sure it's the correct size setTimeout(() => { navigationMapInstance.invalidateSize(); }, 100); } // Restore route from session storage if available const savedRoutePointsJson = sessionStorage.getItem('current_route_points'); if (savedRoutePointsJson) { try { routePoints = JSON.parse(savedRoutePointsJson); // Need to recreate Leaflet markers after deserialization routePoints.forEach(rp => { rp.marker = null; }); // Reset marker object to null updateWaypoints(); getRoute(); } catch (e) { console.error("Failed to load route from session storage:", e); routePoints = []; updateWaypoints(); updateNavigationButtons(); } } else { // If no route in session, check if we should start with current location if (routePoints.length === 0) { getCurrentLocation( (coords) => { // Add current location as the start point addWaypoint({ latitude: coords.latitude, longitude: coords.longitude }); navigationMapInstance.setView([coords.latitude, coords.longitude], 15); showToast("Ubicación actual fijada como punto de partida (S). Pulsa en el mapa para añadir destino o etapas.", "info"); }, (errorMsg) => { showToast(`No se pudo obtener tu ubicación para inicio: ${errorMsg}. Pulsa en el mapa para añadir puntos.`, "warning", 4000); } ); } } const navCloseButton = document.getElementById('nav-close-modal'); if (navCloseButton) { // Ensure only one listener const newNavCloseButton = navCloseButton.cloneNode(true); navCloseButton.parentNode.replaceChild(newNavCloseButton, navCloseButton); newNavCloseButton.addEventListener('click', hideNavigationRouteModal); } const navClearButton = document.getElementById('nav-clear-route'); if (navClearButton) navClearButton.addEventListener('click', clearRoute); const navStartButton = document.getElementById('nav-start-navigation'); if (navStartButton) navStartButton.addEventListener('click', startNavigation); const navStopButton = document.getElementById('nav-stop-navigation'); if (navStopButton) navStopButton.addEventListener('click', stopNavigation); const navSaveButton = document.getElementById('nav-save-route'); if (navSaveButton) navSaveButton.addEventListener('click', saveRoute); const navLoadButton = document.getElementById('nav-load-route'); if (navLoadButton) navLoadButton.addEventListener('click', showSavedRoutesModal); updateNavigationButtons(); // Initial state: navigation not active, info footer hidden document.getElementById('navigation-info-footer').style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('navigation-map-div').classList.remove('navigating'); } function hideNavigationRouteModal() { stopNavigation(); // Stop GPS tracking if active const navModal = document.getElementById('navigation-route-modal'); if (navModal) { navModal.style.display = 'none'; } if (navigationMapInstance) { navigationMapInstance.off('click'); // Remove click listener // Clear all layers navigationMapInstance.eachLayer(layer => { if (layer instanceof L.TileLayer) { // Keep tile layers? Or remove and re-add on next open? Keep for now. } else { layer.remove(); } }); // Keep map instance but clear overlays routePoints = []; routePolyline = null; currentRouteData = null; } // Clear route points from session storage when closing the modal completely sessionStorage.removeItem('current_route_points'); updateNavigationButtons(); document.getElementById('navigation-info-footer').style.display = 'none'; document.getElementById('navigation-map-div').classList.remove('navigating'); // Clear any lingering event listeners on buttons added within the modal const navCloseButton = document.getElementById('nav-close-modal'); if (navCloseButton) { const newNavCloseButton = navCloseButton.cloneNode(true); navCloseButton.parentNode.replaceChild(newNavCloseButton, navCloseButton); } // Remove listeners by replacing const navClearButton = document.getElementById('nav-clear-route'); if (navClearButton) { const newNavClearButton = navClearButton.cloneNode(true); navClearButton.parentNode.replaceChild(newNavClearButton, navClearButton); } const navStartButton = document.getElementById('nav-start-navigation'); if (navStartButton) { const newNavStartButton = navStartButton.cloneNode(true); navStartButton.parentNode.replaceChild(newNavStartButton, navStartButton); } const navStopButton = document.getElementById('nav-stop-navigation'); if (navStopButton) { const newNavStopButton = navStopButton.cloneNode(true); navStopButton.parentNode.replaceChild(newNavStopButton, navStopButton); } const navSaveButton = document.getElementById('nav-save-route'); if (navSaveButton) { const newNavSaveButton = navSaveButton.cloneNode(true); navSaveButton.parentNode.replaceChild(newNavSaveButton, navSaveButton); } const navLoadButton = document.getElementById('nav-load-route'); if (navLoadButton) { const newNavLoadButton = navLoadButton.cloneNode(true); navLoadButton.parentNode.replaceChild(newNavLoadButton, navLoadButton); } } function initializeNavigationMap(mapDivId) { if (navigationMapInstance) { try { navigationMapInstance.remove(); } catch (e) { console.warn("Error removing old nav map instance:", e); } } navigationMapInstance = L.map(mapDivId, { zoomControl: true, center: [40.416775, -3.703790], // Default center (Madrid) zoom: 6, maxZoom: 18 }); L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', { attribution: '© OpenStreetMap contributors' }).addTo(navigationMapInstance); navigationMapInstance.on('click', handleNavigationClick); setTimeout(() => { navigationMapInstance.invalidateSize(); }, 100); } function handleNavigationClick(e) { if (!navigationMapInstance || navigationActive) return; const latlng = e.latlng; if (routePoints.length === 0) { // First click: Start point addWaypoint({ latitude: latlng.lat, longitude: latlng.lng }); } else { // Subsequent clicks: Add waypoint or finish point addWaypoint({ latitude: latlng.lat, longitude: latlng.lng }); } } function addWaypoint(coords, isInitial = false) { if (!coords || typeof coords.latitude !== 'number' || typeof coords.longitude !== 'number') { showToast("Coordenadas inválidas.", "error"); return; } const newPoint = { id: Date.now() + routePoints.length, // Simple unique ID lat: coords.latitude, lng: coords.longitude, type: routePoints.length === 0 ? 'start' : 'waypoint', marker: null // Marker will be created in updateWaypoints }; routePoints.push(newPoint); updateWaypoints(); getRoute(); if (!isInitial) { navigationMapInstance.setView([coords.latitude, coords.longitude], navigationMapInstance.getZoom() > 10 ? navigationMapInstance.getZoom() : 13); } showToast(`Punto ${routePoints.length} añadido.`, 'success', 1000); saveCurrentRoutePoints(); // Save points to session storage } function removeWaypoint(pointId) { const initialLength = routePoints.length; routePoints = routePoints.filter(p => p.id !== pointId); if (routePoints.length < initialLength) { updateWaypoints(); getRoute(); showToast("Punto eliminado.", "info", 1000); saveCurrentRoutePoints(); // Save changes to session storage } } function updateWaypoints() { // Remove existing markers routePoints.forEach(p => { if (p.marker && navigationMapInstance) { p.marker.remove(); } }); // Determine types (S, 1, 2, ..., F) and create new markers routePoints.forEach((point, index) => { let label, className; if (index === 0 && routePoints.length > 1) { label = 'S'; className = 'waypoint-icon start'; point.type = 'start'; } else if (index === routePoints.length - 1 && routePoints.length > 1) { label = 'F'; className = 'waypoint-icon finish'; point.type = 'finish'; } else if (routePoints.length === 1) { label = 'S/F'; // If only one point, it's both start and finish className = 'waypoint-icon start finish'; // Maybe different color? point.type = 'start'; // Treat as start for route calculation simplicity } else { label = (index + 1).toString(); className = 'waypoint-icon waypoint'; point.type = 'waypoint'; } const latlng = L.latLng(point.lat, point.lng); const icon = L.divIcon({ html: `
${label}
×`, className: `leaflet-div-icon ${className}`, iconSize: [30, 30], iconAnchor: [15, 15], }); point.marker = L.marker(latlng, { icon: icon, draggable: !navigationActive // Allow drag in planning mode }).addTo(navigationMapInstance); if (!navigationActive) { // Add dragend listener for repositioning point.marker.on('dragend', (event) => { const newPos = event.target.getLatLng(); point.lat = newPos.lat; point.lng = newPos.lng; // Reorder points if necessary? Or assume only position changes? // For simplicity, just update coordinates and recalculate route getRoute(); saveCurrentRoutePoints(); // Save changes to session storage }); } // Add click listener for removal point.marker.getElement().querySelector('.remove-waypoint').addEventListener('click', (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); // Prevent map click event removeWaypoint(point.id); }); }); updateNavigationButtons(); } function updateNavigationButtons() { const hasRoute = routePoints.length >= 2; const isNavigating = navigationActive; const navSaveButton = document.getElementById('nav-save-route'); const navClearButton = document.getElementById('nav-clear-route'); const navStartButton = document.getElementById('nav-start-navigation'); const navStopButton = document.getElementById('nav-stop-navigation'); if (navSaveButton) navSaveButton.disabled = !hasRoute || isNavigating; if (navClearButton) navClearButton.disabled = routePoints.length === 0 || isNavigating; if (navStartButton) { navStartButton.disabled = !hasRoute || isNavigating; navStartButton.style.display = isNavigating ? 'none' : 'inline-block'; } if (navStopButton) { navStopButton.disabled = !isNavigating; navStopButton.style.display = isNavigating ? 'inline-block' : 'none'; } } async function getRoute() { if (routePoints.length < 2) { if (routePolyline && navigationMapInstance) { routePolyline.remove(); routePolyline = null; } currentRouteData = null; updateNavigationUI(); // Clear UI info updateNavigationButtons(); return; } const waypoints = routePoints.map(p => `${p.lng},${p.lat}`).join(';'); const osrmUrl = `https://router.project-osrm.org/route/v1/driving/${waypoints}?overview=full&geometries=geojson&steps=true`; try { const response = await fetch(osrmUrl); if (!response.ok) { throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`); } const data = await response.json(); if (data.routes && data.routes.length > 0) { currentRouteData = data.routes[0]; if (routePolyline && navigationMapInstance) { routePolyline.remove(); } const geojsonObject = currentRouteData.geometry; routePolyline = L.geoJSON(geojsonObject, { style: { color: '#007bff', weight: 5, opacity: 0.7 } }).addTo(navigationMapInstance); if (!navigationActive) { // Fit bounds only in planning mode navigationMapInstance.fitBounds(routePolyline.getBounds().pad(0.1)); } updateNavigationUI(); updateNavigationButtons(); } else { if (routePolyline && navigationMapInstance) routePolyline.remove(); routePolyline = null; currentRouteData = null; showToast("No se pudo calcular la ruta.", "warning"); updateNavigationUI(); // Clear UI info updateNavigationButtons(); } } catch (error) { if (routePolyline && navigationMapInstance) routePolyline.remove(); routePolyline = null; currentRouteData = null; showToast(`Error al obtener ruta: ${error.message}`, "error"); updateNavigationUI(); // Clear UI info updateNavigationButtons(); } } function updateNavigationUI() { const infoFooter = document.getElementById('navigation-info-footer'); const totalDistanceSpan = document.getElementById('total-distance'); const totalTimeSpan = document.getElementById('total-time'); const etaSpan = document.getElementById('eta'); const remainingDistanceSpan = document.getElementById('remaining-distance'); // Renamed const remainingTimeSpan = document.getElementById('remaining-time'); // Renamed const remainingEtaSpan = document.getElementById('remaining-eta'); // Renamed const nextInstructionDiv = document.getElementById('next-instruction'); const routeProgressBar = document.getElementById('route-progress-bar'); const nextInstructionDistanceBar = document.getElementById('next-instruction-distance-bar'); if (navigationActive && currentRouteData) { infoFooter.style.display = 'flex'; // Update total route info (only once on start) if (totalDistanceSpan) totalDistanceSpan.textContent = `Total: ${formatDistance(currentRouteData.distance)}`; if (totalTimeSpan) totalTimeSpan.textContent = formatDuration(currentRouteData.duration); // Update progress, remaining info, and next instruction dynamically // This will be handled by updateNavigationPosition during navigation if (remainingDistanceSpan) remainingDistanceSpan.textContent = 'Restante: --'; if (remainingTimeSpan) remainingTimeSpan.textContent = '--'; if (remainingEtaSpan) remainingEtaSpan.textContent = 'ETA: --:--'; if (nextInstructionDiv) nextInstructionDiv.textContent = 'Siguiente: ...'; if (routeProgressBar) routeProgressBar.style.width = '0%'; if (nextInstructionDistanceBar) nextInstructionDistanceBar.style.width = '0%'; } else if (currentRouteData) { // Route calculated but not navigating (planning mode) infoFooter.style.display = 'flex'; if (totalDistanceSpan) totalDistanceSpan.textContent = `Total: ${formatDistance(currentRouteData.distance)}`; if (totalTimeSpan) totalTimeSpan.textContent = formatDuration(currentRouteData.duration); if (etaSpan) { const now = new Date(); const etaTime = new Date(now.getTime() + currentRouteData.duration * 1000); etaSpan.textContent = `ETA: ${etaTime.getHours().toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${etaTime.getMinutes().toString().padStart(2, '0')}`; } if (remainingDistanceSpan) remainingDistanceSpan.textContent = 'Restante: -- km'; if (remainingTimeSpan) remainingTimeSpan.textContent = '--'; if (remainingEtaSpan) remainingEtaSpan.textContent = 'ETA: --:--'; if (nextInstructionDiv) nextInstructionDiv.textContent = 'Pulsa "Iniciar Navegación"'; if (routeProgressBar) routeProgressBar.style.width = '0%'; if (nextInstructionDistanceBar) nextInstructionDistanceBar.style.width = '0%'; } else { // No route calculated infoFooter.style.display = 'none'; if (totalDistanceSpan) totalDistanceSpan.textContent = 'Total: -- km'; if (totalTimeSpan) totalTimeSpan.textContent = '--'; if (etaSpan) etaSpan.textContent = 'ETA: --:--'; if (remainingDistanceSpan) remainingDistanceSpan.textContent = 'Restante: -- km'; if (remainingTimeSpan) remainingTimeSpan.textContent = '--'; if (remainingEtaSpan) remainingEtaSpan.textContent = 'ETA: --:--'; if (nextInstructionDiv) nextInstructionDiv.textContent = 'Pulsa en el mapa para añadir puntos.'; if (routeProgressBar) routeProgressBar.style.width = '0%'; if (nextInstructionDistanceBar) nextInstructionDistanceBar.style.width = '0%'; } } function formatDistance(meters) { if (meters < 1000) return `${meters.toFixed(0)} m`; return `${(meters / 1000).toFixed(1)} km`; } function formatDuration(seconds) { const hours = Math.floor(seconds / 3600); const minutes = Math.ceil((seconds % 3600) / 60); if (hours > 0) return `${hours}h ${minutes}min`; return `${minutes}min`; } // OSRM directions narrative helper function getInstructionText(step) { if (!step || !step.maneuver) return 'Continúa...'; const m = step.maneuver; let text = ''; switch (m.type) { case 'turn': text = `Gira ${m.modifier} en ${m.exit ? `la salida ${m.exit}` : ''}${step.name ? ` hacia ${step.name}` : ''}`; break; case 'new name': text = `Continúa hacia ${step.name}`; break; case 'depart': text = `Inicia ruta`; break; case 'arrive': text = `Llegaste a destino`; break; case 'merge': text = `Incorpórate ${m.modifier ? m.modifier : ''}${step.name ? ` hacia ${step.name}` : ''}`; break; case 'fork': text = `Toma ${m.modifier} bifurcación${step.name ? ` hacia ${step.name}` : ''}`; break; case 'roundabout': text = `Toma la ${m.exit}ª salida en la rotonda${step.name ? ` hacia ${step.name}` : ''}`; break; case 'continue': text = `Continúa ${m.modifier ? m.modifier : ''}${step.name ? ` hacia ${step.name}` : ''}`; break; default: text = `${m.type} ${m.modifier ? m.modifier : ''}${step.name ? ` hacia ${step.name}` : ''}`; break; } // Clean up common issues like "hacia undefined" text = text.replace('hacia undefined', '').replace('hacia ', '').replace(' ', ' '); return text.trim(); } function startNavigation() { if (!currentRouteData || routePoints.length < 2) { showToast("No hay ruta válida para iniciar navegación (mínimo 2 puntos).", "warning"); return; } navigationActive = true; currentNavigationStepIndex = 0; currentNavigationLegIndex = 0; // Keep track of current leg (between waypoints) currentNavigationPointIndex = 0; // Keep track of index in current geometry coordinates // Ensure all waypoints are non-draggable during navigation routePoints.forEach(p => { if (p.marker) p.marker.dragging.disable(); }); document.getElementById('navigation-map-div').classList.add('navigating'); document.getElementById('navigation-info-footer').style.display = 'flex'; updateNavigationButtons(); showToast("Navegación iniciada.", "success"); // Start watching user's location if ('geolocation' in navigator && 'watchPosition' in navigator.geolocation) { if (navigationLocationWatchId !== null) { navigator.geolocation.clearWatch(navigationLocationWatchId); } navigationLocationWatchId = navigator.geolocation.watchPosition( (position) => { const coords = { latitude: position.coords.latitude, longitude: position.coords.longitude, accuracy: position.coords.accuracy, heading: position.coords.heading, // heading is direction of travel speed: position.coords.speed // speed in m/s }; updateNavigationPosition(coords); }, (error) => { showToast(`Error seguimiento GPS: ${error.message}`, "error"); // Optionally stop navigation if critical error if (error.code === error.PERMISSION_DENIED || error.code === error.POSITION_UNAVAILABLE) { stopNavigation(); } }, { enableHighAccuracy: true, timeout: 5000, maximumAge: 1000, distanceFilter: 5 } // Adjust options for real-time tracking ); showToast("Iniciando seguimiento GPS...", "info", 2000); } else { showToast("Tu navegador no soporta seguimiento GPS.", "error"); stopNavigation(); } } function stopNavigation() { navigationActive = false; if (navigationLocationWatchId !== null) { navigator.geolocation.clearWatch(navigationLocationWatchId); navigationLocationWatchId = null; } if (navigationUserMarker) { navigationUserMarker.remove(); navigationUserMarker = null; } if (navigationUserCircle) { navigationUserCircle.remove(); navigationUserCircle = null; } // Re-enable marker dragging in planning mode routePoints.forEach(p => { if (p.marker) p.marker.dragging.enable(); }); document.getElementById('navigation-map-div').classList.remove('navigating'); document.getElementById('navigation-info-footer').style.display = 'none'; // Hide info footer updateNavigationButtons(); showToast("Navegación detenida.", "info"); // Reset UI elements in info footer to default state updateNavigationUI(); // Restore route points to session storage on stop, in case user wants to resume planning saveCurrentRoutePoints(); } function updateNavigationPosition(coords) { if (!navigationActive || !navigationMapInstance || !currentRouteData || !coords || typeof coords.latitude !== 'number' || typeof coords.longitude !== 'number') { return; } const latLng = L.latLng(coords.latitude, coords.longitude); // Update user marker and accuracy circle if (navigationUserMarker) { navigationUserMarker.setLatLng(latLng); // Update heading (direction of travel) if available if (coords.heading !== null && !isNaN(coords.heading)) { // Leaflet marker rotation requires transform-origin and transform const markerElement = navigationUserMarker.getElement(); if(markerElement) { markerElement.style.transformOrigin = 'center center'; // Add rotate CSS transform to existing transform // Get current transform (might include scale, etc.) const currentTransform = markerElement.style.transform; const rotationTransform = `rotate(${coords.heading}deg)`; // Remove existing rotation if present const existingRotationMatch = currentTransform.match(/rotate\([^)]*\)/); let newTransform = currentTransform; if (existingRotationMatch) { newTransform = currentTransform.replace(existingRotationMatch[0], '').trim(); } // Combine new rotation with potentially existing other transforms markerElement.style.transform = `${newTransform} ${rotationTransform}`.trim(); } } } else { navigationUserMarker = L.marker(latLng, { icon: carIcon, // Use the car icon zIndexOffset: 10000, // Ensure it's on top rotationAngle: coords.heading !== null && !isNaN(coords.heading) ? coords.heading : 0 // Initial rotation }).addTo(navigationMapInstance); // For browsers that don't support Leaflet's rotationAngle option directly, // manually apply transform like done in the setLatLng block above. if (coords.heading !== null && !isNaN(coords.heading)) { const markerElement = navigationUserMarker.getElement(); if (markerElement) { markerElement.style.transformOrigin = 'center center'; markerElement.style.transform = `rotate(${coords.heading}deg)`; } } } const accuracyRadius = Math.max(coords.accuracy, 5); // Use reported accuracy, minimum 5m if (navigationUserCircle) { navigationUserCircle.setLatLng(latLng).setRadius(accuracyRadius); } else { navigationUserCircle = L.circle(latLng, accuracyRadius, { color: 'blue', fillColor: '#2196F3', fillOpacity: 0.2, weight: 2 }).addTo(navigationMapInstance); } // Center map on user position navigationMapInstance.panTo(latLng); // Update progress and instructions if (currentRouteData && currentRouteData.geometry && currentRouteData.steps) { const routeCoords = L.GeoJSON.coordsToLatLngs(currentRouteData.geometry.coordinates, currentRouteData.geometry.type === 'LineString' ? 0 : 1); // Find closest point on the route to the user's current location const closest = L.GeometryUtil.closest(navigationMapInstance, routeCoords, latLng); if (closest && currentRouteData.geometry.type === 'LineString') { // closest.distance is distance from user to closest point on polyline // closest.index is the index of the coordinate *after* the closest segment starts // closest.latlng is the closest point on the polyline as a LatLng object // Find the current step based on the closest point's index let currentStepIndex = -1; let distanceTravelledOnRoute = 0; let totalRouteDistance = 0; let remainingDistance = 0; let remainingDuration = 0; // Calculate total route distance for progress bar (sum of segment distances) for(let i = 0; i < routeCoords.length - 1; i++) { totalRouteDistance += routeCoords[i].distanceTo(routeCoords[i+1]); } // Find the segment the user is currently on or just passed let segmentStartCoord = null; let segmentEndCoord = null; let segmentDistance = 0; let distanceToClosest = closest.distance; // Calculate distance traveled along the route polyline up to the closest point for(let i = 0; i < closest.originalIndex; i++) { distanceTravelledOnRoute += routeCoords[i].distanceTo(routeCoords[i+1]); } // Add distance along the segment from the start of the segment to the closest point if (closest.originalIndex < routeCoords.length -1) { segmentStartCoord = routeCoords[closest.originalIndex]; segmentEndCoord = routeCoords[closest.originalIndex + 1]; distanceTravelledOnRoute += segmentStartCoord.distanceTo(closest.latlng); } // Calculate total route distance again, perhaps more robustly let totalRouteDistanceAccurate = 0; currentRouteData.legs.forEach(leg => { totalRouteDistanceAccurate += leg.distance; }); // Calculate overall route progress const overallProgress = Math.min(1, distanceTravelledOnRoute / totalRouteDistanceAccurate); if (routeProgressBar) routeProgressBar.style.width = `${overallProgress * 100}%`; // Find the current step and leg let currentLegIndex = 0; let currentStepInLegIndex = 0; let distanceCoveredInLeg = 0; let distanceToClosestInLeg = closest.latlng.distanceTo(routePoints[currentLegIndex].marker.getLatLng()); let foundCurrentStep = false; let totalDistanceBeforeCurrentStep = 0; for (let l = 0; l < currentRouteData.legs.length; l++) { const leg = currentRouteData.legs[l]; let distanceCoveredInThisLeg = 0; for (let s = 0; s < leg.steps.length; s++) { const step = leg.steps[s]; const stepCoords = L.GeoJSON.coordsToLatLngs(step.geometry.coordinates, step.geometry.type === 'LineString' ? 0 : 1); let stepDistance = 0; for(let i = 0; i < stepCoords.length - 1; i++) { stepDistance += stepCoords[i].distanceTo(stepCoords[i+1]); } // Check if closest point is within this step's geometry bounding box (a rough check) const stepBounds = L.latLngBounds(stepCoords); if (stepBounds.contains(closest.latlng) && !foundCurrentStep) { currentLegIndex = l; currentStepInLegIndex = s; currentStepIndex = step.geometry_index; // OSRM's index for the step in the full geometry foundCurrentStep = true; // More precise check: is the closest point on *this* step's polyline? // This requires finding the closest point *on this step's specific geometry* // For simplicity, let's rely on the overall closest point index for now // And assume if the overall closest point index is within the geometry indices range of this step, // the user is on or has just passed this step. // Calculate distance traveled *within* this step's geometry up to the closest point let distanceInCurrentStep = 0; const closestInStep = L.GeometryUtil.closest(navigationMapInstance, stepCoords, latLng); if (closestInStep) { for (let i = 0; i < closestInStep.originalIndex; i++) { distanceInCurrentStep += stepCoords[i].distanceTo(stepCoords[i+1]); } if (closestInStep.originalIndex < stepCoords.length - 1) { distanceInCurrentStep += stepCoords[closestInStep.originalIndex].distanceTo(closestInStep.latlng); } } distanceCoveredInLeg += distanceInCurrentStep; } else if (!foundCurrentStep) { distanceCoveredInLeg += stepDistance; // Add full step distance if not the current step } if (foundCurrentStep) break; // Stop searching steps in this leg if step found totalDistanceBeforeCurrentStep += stepDistance; } if (foundCurrentStep) break; // Stop searching legs if step found distanceCoveredInLeg = leg.distance; // If step wasn't found in this leg, user is past this leg } // Calculate remaining distance and duration from current position (closest point on route) remainingDistance = totalRouteDistanceAccurate - distanceTravelledOnRoute; // Estimate remaining duration (very rough without complex OSRM logic) // Could use average speed or OSRM step durations let remainingDurationEstimate = 0; let totalDuration = 0; currentRouteData.legs.forEach(leg => { totalDuration += leg.duration; }); const durationPerMeter = totalDuration / totalRouteDistanceAccurate; remainingDurationEstimate = remainingDistance * durationPerMeter; const now = new Date(); const remainingEta = new Date(now.getTime() + remainingDurationEstimate * 1000); if (remainingDistanceSpan) remainingDistanceSpan.textContent = `Restante: ${formatDistance(remainingDistance)}`; if (remainingTimeSpan) remainingTimeSpan.textContent = formatDuration(remainingDurationEstimate); if (remainingEtaSpan) remainingEtaSpan.textContent = `ETA: ${remainingEta.getHours().toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${remainingEta.getMinutes().toString().padStart(2, '0')}`; // Find the next relevant instruction (might be the current step's instruction or the next step) let nextInstruction = 'Continúa...'; let nextInstructionDistance = 0; // Distance *along the route* to the maneuver point let distanceCoveredInCurrentStep = 0; if (foundCurrentStep) { const currentStep = currentRouteData.legs[currentLegIndex].steps[currentStepInLegIndex]; // Calculate distance covered within the current step's geometry const stepCoords = L.GeoJSON.coordsToLatLngs(currentStep.geometry.coordinates, currentStep.geometry.type === 'LineString' ? 0 : 1); const closestInStep = L.GeometryUtil.closest(navigationMapInstance, stepCoords, latLng); if (closestInStep) { for (let i = 0; i < closestInStep.originalIndex; i++) { distanceCoveredInCurrentStep += stepCoords[i].distanceTo(stepCoords[i+1]); } if (closestInStep.originalIndex < stepCoords.length - 1) { distanceCoveredInCurrentStep += stepCoords[closestInStep.originalIndex].distanceTo(closestInStep.latlng); } } const stepRemainingDistance = currentStep.distance - distanceCoveredInCurrentStep; // Check if the user is close enough to the end of the current step to show the *next* step's instruction const threshold = 50; // meters threshold to trigger next instruction early if (stepRemainingDistance <= threshold && (currentStepInLegIndex < currentRouteData.legs[currentLegIndex].steps.length - 1 || currentLegIndex < currentRouteData.legs.length - 1)) { // Move to the next instruction if (currentStepInLegIndex < currentRouteData.legs[currentLegIndex].steps.length - 1) { // Next step in the current leg const nextStep = currentRouteData.legs[currentLegIndex].steps[currentStepInLegIndex + 1]; nextInstruction = getInstructionText(nextStep); nextInstructionDistance = nextStep.distance - (threshold - stepRemainingDistance); // Distance from threshold point to maneuver nextInstructionDistance = Math.max(0, nextInstructionDistance); // Ensure it's not negative // Need total distance of the *next* instruction segment for the progress bar const nextStepCoords = L.GeoJSON.coordsToLatLngs(nextStep.geometry.coordinates, nextStep.geometry.type === 'LineString' ? 0 : 1); let totalNextStepDistance = 0; for(let i = 0; i < nextStepCoords.length - 1; i++) { totalNextStepDistance += nextStepCoords[i].distanceTo(nextStepCoords[i+1]); } if (totalNextStepDistance > 0) { const progressInNextStep = (totalNextStepDistance - nextInstructionDistance) / totalNextStepDistance; if (nextInstructionDistanceBar) nextInstructionDistanceBar.style.width = `${progressInNextStep * 100}%`; } else { if (nextInstructionDistanceBar) nextInstructionDistanceBar.style.width = '100%'; // Handle zero-length steps } } else if (currentLegIndex < currentRouteData.legs.length - 1) { // Next leg starts immediately (first step of next leg) const nextLeg = currentRouteData.legs[currentLegIndex + 1]; const nextStep = nextLeg.steps[0]; // First step of the next leg nextInstruction = getInstructionText(nextStep); nextInstructionDistance = nextStep.distance; // Distance is the length of the next step // Distance bar for the first step of the next leg const nextStepCoords = L.GeoJSON.coordsToLatLngs(nextStep.geometry.coordinates, nextStep.geometry.type === 'LineString' ? 0 : 1); let totalNextStepDistance = 0; for(let i = 0; i < nextStepCoords.length - 1; i++) { totalNextStepDistance += nextStepCoords[i].distanceTo(nextStepCoords[i+1]); } if (totalNextStepDistance > 0) { const progressInNextStep = (totalNextStepDistance - nextInstructionDistance) / totalNextStepDistance; if (nextInstructionDistanceBar) nextInstructionDistanceBar.style.width = `${progressInNextStep * 100}%`; } else { if (nextInstructionDistanceBar) nextInstructionDistanceBar.style.width = '100%'; // Handle zero-length steps } } } else { // Still in the current step, show its maneuver or a simple continue const currentStep = currentRouteData.legs[currentLegIndex].steps[currentStepInLegIndex]; nextInstruction = getInstructionText(currentStep); nextInstructionDistance = stepRemainingDistance; // Distance bar for the remaining distance in the current step const stepCoords = L.GeoJSON.coordsToLatLngs(currentStep.geometry.coordinates, currentStep.geometry.type === 'LineString' ? 0 : 1); let totalCurrentStepDistance = 0; for(let i = 0; i < stepCoords.length - 1; i++) { totalCurrentStepDistance += stepCoords[i].distanceTo(stepCoords[i+1]); } if (totalCurrentStepDistance > 0) { const progressInStep = (totalCurrentStepDistance - nextInstructionDistance) / totalCurrentStepDistance; if (nextInstructionDistanceBar) nextInstructionDistanceBar.style.width = `${progressInStep * 100}%`; } else { if (nextInstructionDistanceBar) nextInstructionDistanceBar.style.width = '0%'; // Handle zero-length steps } } } else { // User is potentially off-route or just starting/finishing nextInstruction = 'Recalculando o sin ruta...'; nextInstructionDistance = 0; if (nextInstructionDistanceBar) nextInstructionDistanceBar.style.width = '0%'; } if (nextInstructionDiv) { nextInstructionDiv.textContent = `Siguiente: ${nextInstruction} (${formatDistance(nextInstructionDistance)})`; } // Add stage markers to the progress bar const routeProgressContainer = document.getElementById('route-progress-container'); if (routeProgressContainer && currentRouteData.legs.length > 1) { // Clear existing stage markers routeProgressContainer.querySelectorAll('.stage-marker').forEach(marker => marker.remove()); let cumulativeDistance = 0; for(let i = 0; i < currentRouteData.legs.length - 1; i++) { // Mark points between legs, not the final destination cumulativeDistance += currentRouteData.legs[i].distance; const percentage = (cumulativeDistance / totalRouteDistanceAccurate) * 100; const stageMarker = document.createElement('div'); stageMarker.className = 'stage-marker'; stageMarker.style.left = `${percentage}%`; routeProgressContainer.appendChild(stageMarker); } } } } } function saveCurrentRoutePoints() { if (routePoints.length > 0) { // Store only the necessary data (lat, lng) const serializablePoints = routePoints.map(p => ({ lat: p.lat, lng: p.lng })); sessionStorage.setItem('current_route_points', JSON.stringify(serializablePoints)); } else { sessionStorage.removeItem('current_route_points'); } updateNavigationButtons(); } function clearRoute() { if (navigationActive) stopNavigation(); // Stop navigation first routePoints.forEach(p => { if (p.marker && navigationMapInstance) { p.marker.remove(); } }); if (routePolyline && navigationMapInstance) { routePolyline.remove(); routePolyline = null; } routePoints = []; currentRouteData = null; updateWaypoints(); updateNavigationUI(); updateNavigationButtons(); sessionStorage.removeItem('current_route_points'); // Clear from session storage showToast("Ruta limpia.", "info"); // Reset map view if (navigationMapInstance) { navigationMapInstance.setView([40.416775, -3.703790], 6); // Default center/zoom } // Optional: Re-add current location as start point after clear getCurrentLocation( (coords) => { addWaypoint({ latitude: coords.latitude, longitude: coords.longitude }); navigationMapInstance.setView([coords.latitude, coords.longitude], 15); showToast("Ubicación actual fijada como punto de partida (S).", "info"); }, (errorMsg) => { showToast(`No se pudo obtener tu ubicación para inicio: ${errorMsg}. Pulsa en el mapa para añadir puntos.`, "warning", 4000); } ); } function getSavedRoutes() { try { const routes = localStorage.getItem(ROUTE_STORAGE_KEY); return routes ? JSON.parse(routes) : []; } catch (e) { console.error("Error loading saved routes:", e); return []; } } function saveRoute() { if (!currentRouteData || routePoints.length < 2) { showToast("No hay ruta válida para guardar.", "warning"); return; } let routeName = prompt("Introduce un nombre para la ruta:"); if (!routeName || routeName.trim() === "") { showToast("Nombre de ruta no válido.", "warning"); return; } routeName = routeName.trim(); const savedRoutes = getSavedRoutes(); // Store necessary data: points (lat, lng), maybe route summary? const newRoute = { id: Date.now(), // Unique ID name: routeName, points: routePoints.map(p => ({ lat: p.lat, lng: p.lng })), summary: currentRouteData.summary || 'Ruta guardada', // Use OSRM summary if available distance: currentRouteData.distance || 0, duration: currentRouteData.duration || 0, savedAt: new Date().toISOString() }; savedRoutes.push(newRoute); try { localStorage.setItem(ROUTE_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(savedRoutes)); showToast(`Ruta "${routeName}" guardada.`, "success"); } catch (e) { showToast(`Error al guardar ruta: ${e.message}`, "error"); } } function loadRoute(routeId) { const savedRoutes = getSavedRoutes(); const routeToLoad = savedRoutes.find(r => r.id === routeId); if (!routeToLoad) { showToast("Ruta no encontrada.", "error"); return; } if (navigationActive) stopNavigation(); // Stop current navigation if active // Clear current route clearRoute(); // This also removes markers and polyline // Load points from saved route routePoints = routeToLoad.points.map((p, index) => ({ id: Date.now() + index, // Assign new temporary IDs lat: p.lat, lng: p.lng, type: index === 0 ? 'start' : (index === routeToLoad.points.length - 1 ? 'finish' : 'waypoint'), marker: null })); // Update markers on the map updateWaypoints(); // Recalculate the route with the loaded points getRoute(); // Save the loaded points to session storage saveCurrentRoutePoints(); showToast(`Ruta "${routeToLoad.name}" cargada.`, "success"); // Close the saved routes modal after loading const savedRoutesModal = document.getElementById('saved-routes-modal'); if (savedRoutesModal) { const closeButton = savedRoutesModal.querySelector('#nav-close-saved-routes-modal'); if (closeButton) closeButton.click(); } } function deleteRoute(routeId) { if (navigationActive) stopNavigation(); // Stop navigation if deleting the active route let savedRoutes = getSavedRoutes(); const initialCount = savedRoutes.length; savedRoutes = savedRoutes.filter(r => r.id !== routeId); if (savedRoutes.length < initialCount) { try { localStorage.setItem(ROUTE_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(savedRoutes)); showToast("Ruta borrada.", "success"); // Reload the list in the modal const savedRoutesModal = document.getElementById('saved-routes-modal'); if (savedRoutesModal) { displaySavedRoutes(savedRoutesModal.querySelector('#saved-routes-list')); } } catch (e) { showToast(`Error al borrar ruta: ${e.message}`, "error"); } } else { showToast("Ruta no encontrada para borrar.", "warning"); } } function showSavedRoutesModal() { const existingModal = document.getElementById('saved-routes-modal'); if (existingModal) { clearModalAutoCloseTimer(existingModal, existingModal.querySelector('#nav-close-saved-routes-modal'), 'saved-routes-modal'); existingModal.remove(); } const modal = document.createElement('div'); modal.id = 'saved-routes-modal'; modal.innerHTML = `

Rutas Guardadas

`; document.body.appendChild(modal); const listElement = modal.querySelector('#saved-routes-list'); const closeButton = modal.querySelector('#nav-close-saved-routes-modal'); displaySavedRoutes(listElement); closeButton.addEventListener('click', () => { clearModalAutoCloseTimer(modal, closeButton, 'saved-routes-modal'); modal.remove(); }); addModalAutoCloseTimer(modal, closeButton, 'saved-routes-modal'); } function displaySavedRoutes(listElement) { const savedRoutes = getSavedRoutes(); listElement.innerHTML = ''; if (savedRoutes.length === 0) { listElement.innerHTML = '

No hay rutas guardadas.

'; return; } savedRoutes.forEach(route => { const routeDiv = document.createElement('div'); routeDiv.className = 'location-slot'; // Reusing style class routeDiv.innerHTML = ` ${route.name || 'Ruta sin nombre'} (${formatDistance(route.distance)}, ${formatDuration(route.duration)}) `; listElement.appendChild(routeDiv); routeDiv.querySelector('.load-route-button').addEventListener('click', () => { loadRoute(route.id); }); routeDiv.querySelector('.delete-route-button').addEventListener('click', () => { if (confirm(`¿Seguro que quieres borrar la ruta "${route.name}"?`)) { deleteRoute(route.id); } }); }); } // --- Initialisation and Event Listeners --- async function initializeApp() { isRemindersLocationMapActive = false; renderGrid(); createOtherButtons(); renderToggleButtons(); try { await updateVersion(); } catch (e) { console.error("Error updating version:", e); } loadSavedSettings(); try { await loadNotices(); startNoticeRotation(); } catch (e) { console.error("Error loading notices:", e); } if (reminderCheckIntervalId) { clearInterval(reminderCheckIntervalId); } checkReminders(); // Initial check and interval start // reminderCheckIntervalId = setInterval(checkReminders, currentCheckIntervalDuration); // checkReminders now handles interval start/adjustment const noticeToggleIcon = document.getElementById('notice-toggle-icon'); if (noticeToggleIcon) noticeToggleIcon.addEventListener('click', toggleNotices); const countEl = document.getElementById('reminder-count-globe'); if (countEl) { const openTable = (e) => { if (isEditMode || isAssignmentMode || isKeywordAssignmentMode) return; e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); showAllReminders(); }; countEl.addEventListener('click', openTable); countEl.style.cursor = 'pointer'; } const filterInput = document.getElementById('grid-filter-input'); const clearButton = document.getElementById('clear-filter-button'); if (filterInput) { filterInput.addEventListener('input', () => { localStorage.setItem('gridFilterValue', filterInput.value); filterGridItems(); if(isKeywordAssignmentMode) applyInitialKeywordHighlights(); }); } if (clearButton) { clearButton.addEventListener('click', () => { if (filterInput) filterInput.value = ''; localStorage.removeItem('gridFilterValue'); filterGridItems(); if(isKeywordAssignmentMode) applyInitialKeywordHighlights(); }); } adjustButtonPositions(); window.addEventListener('resize', adjustButtonPositions); checkVersionsIconOpacity(); } document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => { loadCustomData(); storedPin = localStorage.getItem('password_pin'); const savedPasswordActive = localStorage.getItem('password_active'); isPasswordActive = savedPasswordActive ? JSON.parse(savedPasswordActive) : false; if (isPasswordActive && storedPin) { promptForPin(); } else { await initializeApp(); } window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => { if (reminderCheckIntervalId) { clearInterval(reminderCheckIntervalId); } if (locationWatchId !== null) { navigator.geolocation.clearWatch(locationWatchId); locationWatchId = null; } if (navigationLocationWatchId !== null) { navigator.geolocation.clearWatch(navigationLocationWatchId); navigationLocationWatchId = null; } // Clear navigation watch if (editingTargetElement) { editingTargetElement.classList.remove('editing-target'); editingTargetElement = null; } const openReminderModal = document.querySelector('.reminder-modal'); if (openReminderModal && typeof openReminderModal.cleanUpModalTimers === 'function') { openReminderModal.cleanUpModalTimers(true); } Object.keys(globalModalTimers).forEach(modalId => { const timerData = globalModalTimers[modalId]; if (timerData) { clearModalAutoCloseTimer(timerData.modalElement, timerData.closeButtonElement, modalId); } }); globalModalTimers = {}; const openTableModal = document.querySelector('.reminder-table-modal'); if(openTableModal && openTableModal.autoCloseInterval) { clearInterval(openTableModal.autoCloseInterval); } const openPostponeModal = document.getElementById('postpone-options-modal'); if(openPostponeModal && openPostponeModal.autoPostponeInterval) { clearInterval(openPostponeModal.autoPostponeInterval); } const openSavedLocationsModal = document.querySelector('.saved-locations-modal'); if (openSavedLocationsModal && locationPickerMap) { try { locationPickerMap.remove(); } catch(e){} locationPickerMap = null; locationPickerMarker = null; } const openAllLocationsMapModal = document.getElementById('reminders-location-map-modal'); if (openAllLocationsMapModal && allLocationsMapInstance) { if (locationWatchId !== null) { navigator.geolocation.clearWatch(locationWatchId); locationWatchId = null; } try {allLocationsMapInstance.remove();} catch(e){} allLocationsMapInstance = null; initialUserLocationMarker = null; initialUserLocationMarkerLat = null; initialUserLocationMarkerLng = null; if (initialUserLocationCircle) { initialUserLocationCircle.remove(); initialUserLocationCircle = null; } orientationAltitudeControl = null; } const openNavModal = document.getElementById('navigation-route-modal'); if (openNavModal) { // If navigation modal is open, ensure cleanup happens stopNavigation(); // Explicitly stop navigation // Clear any map instance specific to navigation here if needed, but hideNavigationRouteModal should handle this } if (isAssignmentMode || isEditMode || isKeywordAssignmentMode) { saveCustomData(); } const filterInput = document.getElementById('grid-filter-input'); if (filterInput && filterInput.value.trim()) { localStorage.setItem('gridFilterValue', filterInput.value); } else { localStorage.removeItem('gridFilterValue'); } saveSettings(); if (reminderModalMap) try {reminderModalMap.remove();} catch(e){} Object.values(previewMaps).forEach(map => {try {map?.remove();} catch(e){}}); // Save current route points to session storage before closing saveCurrentRoutePoints(); }); });
